<review>Took on downside up room as a group of 2. Were able to make it through the room fairly easily because we have done multiple escape rooms in the past. Again as a group of two, this one was very tricky and we completed it just under the time limit. Again, I like how the clues are laid out. Some of the clues are very slick and and the room / clue flow made sense and was really fun.

A year or two ago I would have given them 5 stars but for the last year my experiences have been very unimpressive and worse.  Their merchandise has been really second rate and their prices have gone up dramatically.  On the rare occasion I find something I want it almost always is cheaper online in new condition compared to torn, dented and stained condition at BullDog.
